The board is a chaotic collage of announcements, requests, and general town gossip. You sift through them, your eyes scanning for anything that catches your attention.

You notice:

*   **Lost Cat:** A plea from a distraught elderly woman named Agnes, offering a reward for the return of her beloved tabby, Mittens. (Illustration of a grumpy-looking cat attached).
*   **Harvest Festival Announcement:** Details about the upcoming annual Harvest Festival, including contests, games, and a grand feast.
*   **Wanted: Skilled Woodcutter:** The local lumber mill is seeking a strong and reliable woodcutter, offering good wages and lodging.
*   **Odd Jobs Available:** A list of small tasks needed around the village, such as mending fences, cleaning gutters, and fetching water.
*   ***"Missing Persons: The Silverstream Family"*** A crudely drawn poster, almost hidden beneath the others. The ink is smudged, and the paper is torn at the edges. It depicts a family of four – a father, mother, and two young children. The handwriting beneath the image is shaky and desperate: *“Last seen heading towards the Whispering Woods. Any information, please contact Elara Silverstream at the old mill."* Barnaby suddenly starts thumping his foot against the ground.

The town square, now observed with a bit more detail as you examined the board, is more lively than you first noticed. Children play tag around the fountain, their laughter echoing through the square. Merchants hawk their wares, their voices blending into a chorus of commerce. A grizzled old man sits on a bench, whittling a piece of wood with a practiced hand. He eyes you with a knowing glance, a hint of amusement in his eyes. The air still carries the delicious scent of baking bread, tempting you to satisfy your appetite. The weather is warm and sunny, but there is a slight breeze that picks up the leaves scattered across the cobblestones.

1.  {Approach Elara Silverstream at the old mill to inquire about the missing family}.
2.  {Investigate the Whispering Woods for any sign of the missing Silverstream family}.
3.  {Offer to help Agnes find her lost cat, Mittens, hoping for a small reward}.
4.  {Attempt to subtly use *Detect Magic* on the missing persons poster}.
5.  {Buy an extra large loaf of bread from the bakery and then attempt to sell slices to the townsfolk}.

1
"Excuse me," you say, smoothing down your robes, "I saw the poster about the missing Silverstream family on the notice board. I might be able to help. Could you direct me to the old mill where I can find Elara?"

The old man whittling on the bench looks up, his eyes crinkling at the corners. "Ah, the Silverstreams... a sad business indeed," he says, pausing his whittling. "Elara's been beside herself with worry. You'll find the old mill on the western edge of town, just before the path leads into the Whispering Woods. Can't miss it – it's the only building that looks like it's about to collapse into a pile of sawdust." He chuckles, then adds, "Poor Elara. She's a good woman. I hope you can bring her some good news."

You thank the old man and, with Barnaby hopping excitedly at your heels, head towards the western edge of Oakhaven. As you walk, you notice that the happy atmosphere of the town square gradually fades, replaced by a more somber mood. The houses become more dilapidated, and the faces of the villagers you pass are etched with concern. The air grows cooler as you approach the Whispering Woods, a sense of unease settling in your stomach.

Finally, you arrive at the old mill. It's a ramshackle structure, its wooden walls weathered and warped, its roof sagging precariously. The water wheel is still and silent, covered in moss and grime. A wisp of smoke curls from the chimney, suggesting that someone is inside. The only sound is the gentle rustling of leaves in the nearby woods and Barnaby nervously thumping one foot.

As you approach the mill, the door creaks open, revealing a woman with tired eyes and disheveled hair. She looks up at you with a flicker of hope in her gaze. "Can I help you?" she asks, her voice trembling slightly. She has a general store apron on but it appears to be covered in dried flour.

1.  {Introduce yourself as a mage who saw the poster and offer your services to find the Silverstream family}.
2.  {Cast *Detect Magic* on Elara to see if she or the mill holds any magical secrets}.
3.  {Politely ask Elara if she knows what her family was doing in the Whispering Woods}.
4.  {Attempt to reassure Elara that you will do everything in your power to help her, emphasizing your magical abilities}.
5.  {Immediately rush past Elara into the mill, shouting "Show me where they kept the treasure!"}
